// js/demo-submission.js

window.DMG_DEMO_SUBMISSION_ENABLED = false;
window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE = {
    phase: 'idle',
    step: 0,
    hydratedStep: -1,
};

window.getDemoSubmissionConfig = function () {
    return window.APP_CONFIG?.DEMO_SUBMISSION?.SCENARIO || null;
};

window.isDemoSubmissionEnabled = function () {
    return window.APP_CONFIG?.DEMO_SUBMISSION?.ENABLED === true &&
        window.DMG_DEMO_SUBMISSION_ENABLED === true;
};

window.stopDemoSubmissionGuide = function () {
    document.removeEventListener('keydown', window.__DMG_DEMO_GUIDE_KEYDOWN__);
    window.__DMG_DEMO_GUIDE_KEYDOWN__ = null;
    window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE.phase = 'idle';
    window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE.step = 0;
    window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE.hydratedStep = -1;
};

window.resetDemoConstraintStep = function () {
    const constraintsList = document.getElementById('constraintsList');
    const firstConstraint = constraintsList?.querySelector('.constraint-item');

    if (firstConstraint) {
        firstConstraint.value = '';
        firstConstraint.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
    }
};

window.resetDemoKnownReferenceUrlStep = function () {
    const referencesList = document.getElementById('referencesList');
    const block = referencesList?.querySelectorAll('.reference-block')?.[0];
    if (!block) return;

    const urlInput = block.querySelector('.reference-url-input');
    const titleInput = block.querySelector('.reference-title-input');
    const noteInput = block.querySelector('.reference-note-input');
    const bottomRow = block.querySelector('.reference-row-bottom');
    const warningText = block.querySelector('.reference-warning-text');
    const fetchIndicator = block.querySelector('.reference-fetch-indicator');

    if (urlInput) {
        urlInput.value = '';
        urlInput.dataset.lastUrl = '';
    }
    if (titleInput) {
        titleInput.value = '';
        titleInput.readOnly = false;
        titleInput.classList.remove('title-locked');
    }
    if (noteInput) {
        noteInput.value = '';
        noteInput.classList.add('u-hidden');
    }
    if (bottomRow) bottomRow.classList.add('u-hidden');
    if (warningText) {
        warningText.textContent = '';
        warningText.classList.add('u-hidden');
    }
    if (fetchIndicator) fetchIndicator.classList.add('u-hidden');
};

window.resetDemoKnownReferenceNoteStep = function () {
    const referencesList = document.getElementById('referencesList');
    const block = referencesList?.querySelectorAll('.reference-block')?.[0];
    if (!block) return;

    const noteInput = block.querySelector('.reference-note-input');
    if (noteInput) {
        noteInput.value = '';
        noteInput.classList.add('u-hidden');
    }
};

window.resetDemoUnknownReferenceUrlStep = function () {
    const referencesList = document.getElementById('referencesList');
    const block = referencesList?.querySelectorAll('.reference-block')?.[1];
    if (!block) return;

    const urlInput = block.querySelector('.reference-url-input');
    const titleInput = block.querySelector('.reference-title-input');
    const noteInput = block.querySelector('.reference-note-input');
    const bottomRow = block.querySelector('.reference-row-bottom');
    const warningText = block.querySelector('.reference-warning-text');
    const fetchIndicator = block.querySelector('.reference-fetch-indicator');

    if (urlInput) {
        urlInput.value = '';
        urlInput.dataset.lastUrl = '';
    }
    if (titleInput) {
        titleInput.value = '';
        titleInput.readOnly = false;
        titleInput.classList.remove('title-locked');
    }
    if (noteInput) {
        noteInput.value = '';
        noteInput.classList.add('u-hidden');
    }
    if (bottomRow) bottomRow.classList.add('u-hidden');
    if (warningText) {
        warningText.textContent = '';
        warningText.classList.add('u-hidden');
    }
    if (fetchIndicator) fetchIndicator.classList.add('u-hidden');
};

window.resetDemoUnknownReferenceTitleStep = function () {
    const referencesList = document.getElementById('referencesList');
    const block = referencesList?.querySelectorAll('.reference-block')?.[1];
    if (!block) return;

    const titleInput = block.querySelector('.reference-title-input');
    const noteInput = block.querySelector('.reference-note-input');

    if (titleInput) {
        titleInput.value = '';
        titleInput.readOnly = false;
        titleInput.classList.remove('title-locked');
        titleInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
    }

    if (noteInput) {
        noteInput.value = '';
        noteInput.classList.add('u-hidden');
    }
};

window.resetDemoCadenceCountStep = function () {
    const cadenceCountInput = document.getElementById('cadenceCount');
    if (!cadenceCountInput) return;

    cadenceCountInput.value = '1';
    cadenceCountInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
};

window.resetDemoCadenceUnitStep = function () {
    const cadenceUnitSelect = document.getElementById('cadenceUnit');
    const cadenceGroup = document.getElementById('cadenceGroup');

    if (cadenceUnitSelect) cadenceUnitSelect.value = '';
    if (cadenceGroup) cadenceGroup.classList.add('u-hidden');

    window.DMG_SUBMIT_FORM_DEPS?.updateDynamicFields?.();
};

window.resetDemoRecurrenceDurationStep = function () {
    const recurrenceDurationCountInput = document.getElementById('recurrenceDurationCount');
    if (!recurrenceDurationCountInput) return;

    recurrenceDurationCountInput.value = '1';
    recurrenceDurationCountInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
};

window.prefillDemoSubmissionForm = async function () {
    const deps = window.DMG_SUBMIT_FORM_DEPS;
    if (!deps || !window.isDemoSubmissionEnabled?.()) return;

    window.stopDemoSubmissionGuide();
    window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE.phase = 'form';
    window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE.step = 0;

    window.__DMG_DEMO_GUIDE_KEYDOWN__ = async function (e) {
        if (!window.isDemoSubmissionEnabled?.()) return;

        if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') {
            e.preventDefault();
            await window.advanceDemoSubmissionGuide();
        }

        if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft') {
            e.preventDefault();
            await window.rewindDemoSubmissionGuide();
        }
    };

    document.addEventListener('keydown', window.__DMG_DEMO_GUIDE_KEYDOWN__);
    await window.renderDemoSubmissionGuideStep(0);
};

window.advanceDemoSubmissionGuide = async function () {
    const state = window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE;

    if (state.phase === 'form') {
        if (state.step < 11) {
            state.step += 1;
            await window.renderDemoSubmissionGuideStep(state.step);
            return;
        }

        if (state.step === 11) {
            state.phase = 'waiting-submit';
            const submitButton = document.getElementById('submitButton');
            submitButton?.click();
            return;
        }
    }

    if (state.phase === 'success') {
        if (state.step < 15) {
            state.step += 1;
            await window.renderDemoSubmissionGuideStep(state.step);
        }
    }
};

window.rewindDemoSubmissionGuide = async function () {
    const state = window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE;

    if (state.phase === 'form') {
        const deps = window.DMG_SUBMIT_FORM_DEPS;
        if (!deps) return;

        const {
            goalInput,
            instructionsInput,
            challengeDurationTypeHidden,
            durationCards,
            updateDynamicFields
        } = deps;

        if (state.step === 11) {
            window.resetDemoRecurrenceDurationStep();
        } else if (state.step === 10) {
            window.resetDemoCadenceUnitStep();
        } else if (state.step === 9) {
            window.resetDemoCadenceCountStep();
        } else if (state.step === 8) {
            window.resetDemoUnknownReferenceTitleStep();
        } else if (state.step === 7) {
            window.resetDemoUnknownReferenceUrlStep();
        } else if (state.step === 6) {
            window.resetDemoKnownReferenceNoteStep();
        } else if (state.step === 5) {
            window.resetDemoKnownReferenceUrlStep();
        } else if (state.step === 4) {
            window.resetDemoConstraintStep();
        } else if (state.step === 3) {
            goalInput.value = '';
            instructionsInput.value = '';
            instructionsInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        } else if (state.step === 2) {
            goalInput.value = '';
            goalInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        } else if (state.step === 1) {
            challengeDurationTypeHidden.value = '';
            durationCards.forEach(card => card.classList.remove('selected'));

            challengeTextGroup.classList.add('form-section-disabled');
            cadenceGroup.classList.add('u-hidden');

            updateDynamicFields();
        }

        if (state.step > 0) {
            state.step -= 1;
            state.hydratedStep = state.step - 1;
            updateDynamicFields();
        }

        return;
    }

    if (state.phase === 'success') {
        if (state.step > 13) {
            state.step -= 1;
            await window.renderDemoSubmissionGuideStep(state.step);
        }
    }
};

window.handleDemoSubmissionSuccess = async function () {
    const guide = window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE;
    if (!guide || guide.phase !== 'waiting-submit') return;

    guide.phase = 'success';
    guide.step = 12;
};

window.renderDemoSubmissionGuideStep = async function (step) {
    const demo = window.getDemoSubmissionConfig?.();
    const deps = window.DMG_SUBMIT_FORM_DEPS;

    if (!demo || !deps) return;

    const {
        goalInput,
        instructionsInput,
        constraintsList,
        referencesList,
        challengeDurationTypeHidden,
        durationCards,
        challengeTextGroup,
        cadenceGroup,
        cadenceUnitSelect,
        cadenceCountInput,
        recurrenceDurationCountInput,
        generateConstraintInput,
        generateReferenceRow,
        setupReferenceBlockListeners,
        setCadenceTimeframeDefaults,
        updateDynamicFields
    } = deps;

    const state = window.DMG_DEMO_GUIDE || { hydratedStep: -1 };

    const wait = (ms) => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

    const scrollSubmitFormToBottom = async () => {
        const submitButton = document.getElementById('submitButton');
        const formFooter = document.querySelector('.form-footer-actions');
        const targetEl = submitButton || formFooter;

        await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
        await new Promise(resolve => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));

        if (!targetEl) return;

        targetEl.scrollIntoView({
            behavior: 'smooth',
            block: 'end'
        });

        await wait(210);
    };

    const appendReferenceBlock = () => {
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
        wrapper.innerHTML = generateReferenceRow();
        const block = wrapper.firstElementChild;
        referencesList.appendChild(block);
        setupReferenceBlockListeners(block);
        return block;
    };

    const getReferenceBlocks = () => Array.from(referencesList.querySelectorAll('.reference-block'));

    const ensureKnownReferenceBlock = () => {
        const blocks = getReferenceBlocks();
        if (blocks[0]) return blocks[0];
        return appendReferenceBlock();
    };

    const ensureUnknownReferenceBlock = () => {
        const blocks = getReferenceBlocks();
        if (blocks[1]) return blocks[1];
        return appendReferenceBlock();
    };

    const ensurePlaceholderReferenceBlock = () => {
        const blocks = getReferenceBlocks();
        if (blocks[2]) return blocks[2];
        return appendReferenceBlock();
    };

    const fillKnownReference = async () => {
        const ref = demo.references?.[0];
        if (!ref) return;

        const block = ensureKnownReferenceBlock();
        const typeSelect = block.querySelector('.reference-type-select');
        const urlInput = block.querySelector('.reference-url-input');
        const titleInput = block.querySelector('.reference-title-input');
        const bottomRow = block.querySelector('.reference-row-bottom');

        if (typeSelect) typeSelect.value = ref.type || 'VIDEO';
        if (bottomRow) bottomRow.classList.remove('u-hidden');

        if (titleInput?.value?.trim()) return;

        if (urlInput && urlInput.value !== (ref.url || '')) {
            urlInput.value = ref.url || '';
            urlInput.dataset.lastUrl = '';
            urlInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
            await wait(700);
        }
    };

    const fillKnownReferenceNote = () => {
        const ref = demo.references?.[0];
        if (!ref) return;

        const block = ensureKnownReferenceBlock();
        const noteInput = block.querySelector('.reference-note-input');

        if (noteInput) {
            noteInput.classList.remove('u-hidden');
            noteInput.value = ref.note || '';
            noteInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        }
    };

    const fillUnknownReferenceUrl = async () => {
        const ref = demo.references?.[1];
        if (!ref) return;

        const block = ensureUnknownReferenceBlock();
        const typeSelect = block.querySelector('.reference-type-select');
        const urlInput = block.querySelector('.reference-url-input');
        const titleInput = block.querySelector('.reference-title-input');
        const bottomRow = block.querySelector('.reference-row-bottom');

        if (typeSelect) typeSelect.value = ref.type || 'VIDEO';
        if (bottomRow) bottomRow.classList.remove('u-hidden');

        if ((urlInput?.value || '') === (ref.url || '') && titleInput?.value?.trim()) return;

        if (urlInput && urlInput.value !== (ref.url || '')) {
            urlInput.value = ref.url || '';
            urlInput.dataset.lastUrl = '';
            urlInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
            await wait(700);
        }
    };

    const fillUnknownReferenceTitle = () => {
        const ref = demo.references?.[1];
        if (!ref) return;

        const block = ensureUnknownReferenceBlock();
        const titleInput = block.querySelector('.reference-title-input');

        if (titleInput) {
            titleInput.readOnly = false;
            titleInput.classList.remove('title-locked');
            titleInput.value = ref.title || '';
            titleInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        }
    };

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 0 && step >= 1) {
        challengeDurationTypeHidden.value = demo.durationType;
        durationCards.forEach(card => {
            card.classList.toggle(
                'selected',
                card.getAttribute('data-duration') === demo.durationType
            );
        });

        challengeTextGroup.classList.remove('form-section-disabled');
        challengeTextGroup.querySelectorAll('input, textarea, select, button').forEach(i => {
            i.disabled = false;
        });

        updateDynamicFields();
        state.hydratedStep = 1;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 2 && step >= 2) {
        goalInput.value = demo.goal || '';
        goalInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        state.hydratedStep = 2;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 3 && step >= 3) {
        instructionsInput.value = demo.instructions || '';
        instructionsInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        state.hydratedStep = 3;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 4 && step >= 4) {
        const firstConstraint = constraintsList.querySelector('.constraint-item');
        if (firstConstraint) {
            firstConstraint.value = demo.constraints?.[0] || '';
            firstConstraint.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        }

        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 4;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 5 && step >= 5) {
        await fillKnownReference();
        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 5;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 6 && step >= 6) {
        fillKnownReferenceNote();
        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 6;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 7 && step >= 7) {
        await fillUnknownReferenceUrl();
        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 7;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 8 && step >= 8) {
        fillUnknownReferenceTitle();
        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 8;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 9 && step >= 9) {
        ensurePlaceholderReferenceBlock();
        cadenceGroup.classList.remove('u-hidden');
        cadenceCountInput.disabled = false;
        cadenceCountInput.value = String(demo.cadenceCount ?? 1);
        cadenceCountInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 9;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 10 && step >= 10) {
        cadenceUnitSelect.disabled = false;
        cadenceUnitSelect.value = demo.cadenceUnit || 'WEEKLY';
        setCadenceTimeframeDefaults(cadenceUnitSelect.value);

        cadenceCountInput.value = String(demo.cadenceCount ?? 1);
        cadenceCountInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));

        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 10;
    }

    if ((state.hydratedStep ?? -1) < 11 && step >= 11) {
        recurrenceDurationCountInput.disabled = false;
        recurrenceDurationCountInput.value = String(demo.recurrenceDurationCount ?? 2);
        recurrenceDurationCountInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        await scrollSubmitFormToBottom();
        state.hydratedStep = 11;
    }

    if (step === 13) {
        const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('challengeDetailsToggleBtn');
        const contentWrapper = document.getElementById('challengeDetailsContentWrapper');
        const detailsContent = document.getElementById('challengeDetailsContent');

        if (toggleBtn && contentWrapper?.classList.contains('u-hidden')) {
            toggleBtn.click();
            await wait(500);
        }

        if (detailsContent) {
            detailsContent.scrollTop = 0;
            await wait(50);

            detailsContent.scrollTo({
                top: detailsContent.scrollHeight,
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });

            await wait(2000);
        }
    }

    if (step === 14) {
        const successStep = document.getElementById('step3_header');

        if (successStep) {
            successStep.scrollIntoView({
                behavior: 'smooth',
                block: 'start'
            });

            await wait(1000);
        }
    }

    if (step === 15) {
        const copyBtn = document.getElementById('copyChallengeLinkBtn');
        copyBtn?.click();
        state.phase = 'done';
    }

    updateDynamicFields();
};

// js/stream-state.js
// This module manages the state of the stream (live/offline) and provides a subscription mechanism for other parts of the app to react to changes in stream status.

window.StreamState = (() => {
    let isStreamLive = false;
    let lastPayload = null;
    let refreshInterval = null;
    const subscribers = new Set();

    function getHeaderElements() {
        return {
            streamStatusText: document.getElementById('streamStatusText'),
            streamStatusIndicator: document.getElementById('streamStatusIndicator')
        };
    }

    function getHeaderConfig() {
        const header = document.querySelector('site-header');

        return {
            liveText: header?.dataset.streamLiveText || 'LIVE',
            offlineText: header?.dataset.streamOfflineText || 'OFFLINE'
        };
    }

    function renderHeader(status) {
        const { streamStatusText, streamStatusIndicator } = getHeaderElements();
        if (!streamStatusText || !streamStatusIndicator) return;

        const { liveText, offlineText } = getHeaderConfig();

        streamStatusIndicator.classList.remove('is-live', 'is-offline');
        streamStatusIndicator.classList.add(status ? 'is-live' : 'is-offline');
        streamStatusText.textContent = status ? liveText : offlineText;
    }

    function notify() {
        subscribers.forEach(callback => {
            try {
                callback(isStreamLive, lastPayload);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('StreamState subscriber error:', error);
            }
        });

        if (window.refreshContextualCtas) {
            window.refreshContextualCtas(isStreamLive);
        }
    }

    async function fetchStatus() {
        try {
            const apiBaseUrl = window.API_BASE_URL || window.getApiBaseUrl?.() || '';
            const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/stream/stats`);
            const data = await response.json();

            isStreamLive = data.isStreamLive === true;
            lastPayload = data;

            renderHeader(isStreamLive, data);
            notify();

            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Stream status sync failed:', error);

            isStreamLive = false;
            lastPayload = null;

            renderHeader(false);
            notify();

            return null;
        }
    }

    function subscribe(callback, { immediate = true } = {}) {
        if (typeof callback !== 'function') return () => {};

        subscribers.add(callback);

        if (immediate) {
            callback(isStreamLive, lastPayload);
        }

        return () => {
            subscribers.delete(callback);
        };
    }

    function startAutoRefresh(
        intervalMs = window.APP_CONFIG?.STREAM_STATUS_REFRESH_MS ?? 42000
    ) {
        stopAutoRefresh();
        refreshInterval = setInterval(fetchStatus, intervalMs);
    }

    function stopAutoRefresh() {
        if (refreshInterval) {
            clearInterval(refreshInterval);
            refreshInterval = null;
        }
    }

    function getState() {
        return {
            isStreamLive,
            lastPayload
        };
    }

    return {
        fetchStatus,
        subscribe,
        startAutoRefresh,
        stopAutoRefresh,
        getState
    };
})();

// js/typewriter.js

window.runTypewriter = function ({
    container,
    text,
    onComplete,
    typo = true,
    minDelay = 42,
    maxDelay = 105,
    pauseDelay = 120,
    endPause = 420
}) {
    const config = window.APP_CONFIG || {};
    const isFast = config.FAST_VERIFICATION === true;
    const isDebug = config.TYPEWRITER_DEBUG === true;

    if (!container) {
        if (isDebug) console.warn('[typewriter] missing container');
        return;
    }

    if (isDebug) {
        console.log('[typewriter] start', {
            text,
            typo,
            isFast,
            container
        });
    }

    if (isFast) {
        container.innerHTML = `<div class="typewriter-container"><div class="typewriter-target"></div></div>`;
        const target = container.querySelector('.typewriter-target');

        if (!target) {
            if (isDebug) console.warn('[typewriter] target creation failed in fast mode');
            return;
        }

        target.textContent = text;

        if (isDebug) console.log('[typewriter] fast mode complete');

        if (onComplete) onComplete();
        return;
    }

    container.innerHTML = `<div class="typewriter-container"><div class="typewriter-target"></div></div>`;
    const target = container.querySelector('.typewriter-target');

    if (!target) {
        if (isDebug) console.warn('[typewriter] target creation failed');
        return;
    }

    const type = (n = 0) => {
        if (n < text.length) {
            const typoIndex = text.indexOf('@') - 1;
            const hasTypoOccurred = target.getAttribute('data-typo') === 'true';

            let delay = Math.floor(Math.random() * (maxDelay - minDelay + 1)) + minDelay;
            if (text.charAt(n) === ' ' || text.charAt(n) === ':') delay += pauseDelay;

            if (typo && n === typoIndex && !hasTypoOccurred) {
                if (isDebug) console.log('[typewriter] typo injected at index', n);

                target.innerHTML = text.substring(0, n) + 'q';
                target.setAttribute('data-typo', 'true');

                setTimeout(() => {
                    target.innerHTML = text.substring(0, n);
                    setTimeout(() => type(n), endPause);
                }, 210);

                return;
            }

            target.innerHTML = text.substring(0, n + 1);
            setTimeout(() => type(n + 1), delay);
        } else {
            if (isDebug) console.log('[typewriter] complete');

            if (onComplete) {
                setTimeout(onComplete, endPause);
            }
        }
    };

    type();
};
